Hide of the Nemean Lion
Hide of the Nemean Lion

The Nemean Lion was the offspring of Typhon and Echidna. It was a vicious beast with an impenetrable hide that ravaged the countryside around Nemea. King Eurystheus ordered Heracles to slay the beast and return with its hide as the first of twelve labors.
Heracles stalked the creature well into the afternoon, until he finally came upon it unnoticed. He fired two arrows at the beast, but the impenetrable hide turned them away harmlessly. The lion charged Heracles, who struck it in the head with his mighty olive-wood club. The club shattered, but the blow managed to daze the lion long enough for him to grab the lion by the throat and choke the life out of it.
Nothing in Heracles' possession was strong enough to skin the hide, so he used the Nemean Lion's own claws. He wore the hide as a cloak, which granted him the same protection as its previous owner.

Athame Keris
Athame Keris

An athame keris is a ceremonial dagger, one of several magical tools used in neopagan religions and other Witchcraft traditions. The creation is a long and complicated Magical ritual which involves the blending of the metal with magickal ingredients and the invoking of a powerful jinn/khodam spirit into the keris Blade. What gives the keris its power is the genie( Also known as Khodam or Jinn) that resides in it. The genie, or jinn, is a magickal spirit that normally exists in a parallel dimension. The performance of complex rituals can draw one across the threshold and encourage it to make its home in a magically prepared object. After the athame keris has been created, the spirit is continually fed, so it gradually grows more powerful. They are often passed down from generation to generation.

zlin201
Leiomano
Leiomano

This weapon uses wood, cord, and shark teeth. Shark teeth fastened in place with a twine of sorts. And while shark teeth are great for ripping up soft flesh, they would not survive an impact with a hard place, much less the leather thong or twine holding it in place. The teeth are aligned just right so that any blow from this, glancing, pulling, cleaving, etc would almost certainly draw blood. And while it might not be as effective as a sword, you better believe that a battle with combatants taking repeated hits from this would get torn to shreds and bleed to death.

And if you take into account that the heavy wooden head could probably deliver pretty hefty blows all by itself, even without the benefit of shark teeth, you can see how this would make for a very effective melee weapon.

STATISTICS:

THACO:  +3 bonus
Damage:  1D6 +3
Damage type piercing
Weight: 3 
Speed Factor: 4
Type:  1-handed
Requires: 5 Strength
5 Dexterity

zlin202
Mere Pounamu
Mere Pounamu

A mere is a short club normally made of a heavy hardwood or stone, such as jade. Shaped like a short paddle and broad and flat at the striking end and with a maximum of two or three grooves on the handle end which also had a hole to allow a wrist-cord to be attached. Due to its hardness, the greenstone mere was always ground much more thinly than those of whalebone or stone and when held against the light, the thin edges have a translucent glow, making a beautiful and also fearsome weapon. Of all the short weapons made of wood stone or bone, the mere pounamu was held in the highest regard. Ancient mere were often carved from the prized inanga variety of jade. Mere vary in length but are generally around 30 cm (12 inches) in length. Mere have two almost flat sides and a rounded, sharpened top. hese were symbols of chieftainship and passed down as valuable heirlooms. Traditionally individual mere are named, and each is said to possess a spirit of its own.

A warrior would use the club in either hand, wielding it like a cleaver with a slicing motion to strike at an adversary's head or neck. When not in use, the mere was carried tucked into the folds of the user's belt, safe yet always at hand.

STATISTICS:
Special: Can kill with a single blow and sometimes knocks enemies unconscious
THACO:  +1 bonus
Damage:  1D6 +1
Damage type piercing
Weight: 3 
Speed Factor: 4
Type:  1-handed
Requires: 5 Strength
Mere Pounamu

A mere is a short club normally made of a heavy hardwood or stone, such as jade. Shaped like a short paddle and broad and flat at the striking end and with a maximum of two or three grooves on the handle end which also had a hole to allow a wrist-cord to be attached. Due to its hardness, the greenstone mere was always ground much more thinly than those of whalebone or stone and when held against the light, the thin edges have a translucent glow, making a beautiful and also fearsome weapon. Of all the short weapons made of wood stone or bone, the mere pounamu was held in the highest regard. Ancient mere were often carved from the prized inanga variety of jade. Mere vary in length but are generally around 30 cm (12 inches) in length. Mere have two almost flat sides and a rounded, sharpened top. hese were symbols of chieftainship and passed down as valuable heirlooms. Traditionally individual mere are named, and each is said to possess a spirit of its own.

A warrior would use the club in either hand, wielding it like a cleaver with a slicing motion to strike at an adversary's head or neck. When not in use, the mere was carried tucked into the folds of the user's belt, safe yet always at hand.

Macuahuitl
Macuahuitl

The "hungry-wood", is essentially a wooden sword with sharp prismatic obsidian blades embedded into its sides. A blow from such a weapon was reputedly capable of decapitating a horse. Although it is sometimes referred to as a sword or club, but it lacks a true equivalent.

The macuahuitl was 3 to 4 feet (0.91 to 1.2 m) long, and three inches (80 mm) broad, with a groove along either edge, into which sharp-edged pieces of flint or obsidian were inserted, and firmly fixed with some adhesive compound. The rows of obsidian blades were sometimes discontinuous, leaving gaps along the side while at other times the rows were set close together and formed a single edge. The design of the macuahuitl allowed the warrior to injure the opponent with the obsidian blades while the blunt top could be used to render an individual unconscious for easy capture and later sacrifice.

The macuahuitl also has some drawbacks. It takes more time to lift and swing a club than it does to thrust with a sword. More space is needed as well,

Tepoztopilli
Tepoztopilli

The tepoztopilli was a pole-arm, roughly the height of a man, with a broad wooden head about twice the length of the users' palm or shorter, edged with razor-sharp obsidian blades which were deeply set in grooves carved into the head, and cemented in place with bitumen or plant resin as an adhesive. This made the weapon vaguely similar to the macuahuitl or "macana", however it had a much smaller cutting edge and a longer handle. This gave the weapon a superior reach, but blows had to be more carefully executed. Halfway between a halberd and a spear, the tepoztopilli was equally useful for slashing and thrusting.

zlin212
Green Dragon Crescent Blade
Green Dragon Crescent Blade

It has gone by many names, the Green dragon saber, black moon dragon, blue dragon moon, cresent glaive, and was copied in the making of the Yellow Dragon. It is also sometimes referred to as the Frost Fair Blade, from the idea that during a battle in the snow, the blade continuously had blood on it. The blood froze and made a layer of frost on the blade. The story of the blade was that the moment the blade was going to be forged by a blacksmith, there was a rising wind and gathering clouds and then suddenly 1780 drops of blood dripped from the air and a green dragon passed by. The dragon was cut up and the body became part of the components for the weapn, making it magical.

Little else is known about the weapon's origin besides the fact that it started out as a basic great blade that belonged to a courageous warrior by the name of Guan Yu. No one is quite sure on how it ended up in the tomb or how it was acquired, but it is said to be infused with the bones of the spirit beast. Supposedly, whoever holds it can feel the power from the creature within their hands, and also the spiritual courage of Guan Yu raging through their entire bodies during battle. The piercing force of the Green Dragon Crescent Blade is devastating to even the largest of opponents. Big or small, all will feel its sting and be brought to their humblest of states. Many have made the mistake of letting the power of the weapon consume them to the point where they feel invincible. Its legend is eternal, mortal man is not.

zlin245
Magical Golden Horseshoe
Magical Golden Horseshoe

A horseshoe is a U-shaped item made of metal or of modern synthetic materials, nailed or glued to the hooves of horses and some other draught animals. Like a shoe on a human, it is used to protect the animal's feet from wear and tear. Professional horseshoers, also called farriers or blacksmiths, attach horseshoes on the palmar surface of the hoof, usually by nailing through the insensitive hoof wall, which is anatomically similar to the human toenail, though much larger and thicker. 

Some horseshoes are crafted from magical elements and give small blessing to the people that wear them as amulets. Because the skill to make such fine items is rare, and components change a little in different regions, the magical benefits vary but such things are an art not science.

zlin263
Rapier of Inigo Montoya
Rapier of Inigo Montoya

When Inigo Montoya's father, Domingo, was asked by a nobleman, with a six-fingered right hand, Count Rugen, to forge a sword to accommodate his unusual grip, Domingo poured his heart and soul into the project. When Rugen returned, he reneged on his promised price. Thus Domingo refused to sell him the sword, not as a matter of money, but because Rugen could not appreciate the great work of the sword. He proclaimed that the sword would now belong to Inigo. Angered, Rugen killed Domingo. Ten-year-old Inigo witnessed the crime and challenged Rugen to a fight, wherein Rugen easily disarmed Inigo, spared his life and allowed him to keep the sword, but scarred his face as a deterrent to further displays of bravery.

Devastated by the loss of his father, Inigo devoted his entire life to becoming a great swordsman in order to avenge his father. His training started when he was 12 years old and included tutelage under the most skilled and savage fencing masters of his time. After 10 years of training, Inigo had become the greatest swordsman of his generation, and the only living man to hold the rank of "wizard" (a fictional fencing rank above "master"). His original elaborate fantasies of revenge eventually evolved into a simple greeting: "Hello. My name is Inigo Montoya. You killed my father. Prepare to die." When he finally confronted Rugen, he repeated the line throughout the duel before at last avenging his father.

Special:
Protection against hold
Attack Speed Modifier: +1
Extra attack per round
Movement Modifer: +1
Rapier of Inigo Montoya

When Inigo Montoya's father, Domingo, was asked by a nobleman, with a six-fingered right hand, Count Rugen, to forge a sword to accommodate his unusual grip, Domingo poured his heart and soul into the project. When Rugen returned, he reneged on his promised price. Thus Domingo refused to sell him the sword, not as a matter of money, but because Rugen could not appreciate the great work of the sword. He proclaimed that the sword would now belong to Inigo. Angered, Rugen killed Domingo. Ten-year-old Inigo witnessed the crime and challenged Rugen to a fight, wherein Rugen easily disarmed Inigo, spared his life and allowed him to keep the sword, but scarred his face as a deterrent to further displays of bravery.

Devastated by the loss of his father, Inigo devoted his entire life to becoming a great swordsman in order to avenge his father. His training started when he was 12 years old and included tutelage under the most skilled and savage fencing masters of his time. After 10 years of training, Inigo had become the greatest swordsman of his generation, and the only living man to hold the rank of "wizard" (a fictional fencing rank above "master"). His original elaborate fantasies of revenge eventually evolved into a simple greeting: "Hello. My name is Inigo Montoya. You killed my father. Prepare to die." When he finally confronted Rugen, he repeated the line throughout the duel before at last avenging his father.

Special:
Protection against hold
Attack Speed Modifier: +1
Extra attack per round
Movement Modifer: +1

Tores

He owned six magical swords and a powerful suit of armor that was impervious to all but the most powerful of magic.     We will have our peace once more when One becomes the Five."

zlin279
Tender Hands of Masamune
Tender Hands of Masamune

A legend tells of a test where Muramasa challenged his master, Masamune, to see who could make a finer sword. They both worked tirelessly and eventually, when both swords were finished, they decided to test the results. The contest was for each to suspend the blades in a small creek with the cutting edge facing the current. Muramasa's sword, the Juuchi Yosamu (10,000 Cold Nights) cut everything that passed its way; fish, leaves floating down the river, the very air which blew on it. Highly impressed with his pupil's work, Masamune lowered his sword, the Yawarakai-Te (Tender Hands), into the current and waited patiently. Not a leaf was cut, the fish swam right up to it, and the air hissed as it gently blew by the blade. After a while, Muramasa began to scoff at his master for his apparent lack of skill in the making of his sword. Smiling to himself, Masamune pulled up his sword, dried it, and sheathed it. All the while, Muramasa was heckling him for his sword's inability to cut anything. A monk, who had been watching the whole ordeal, walked over and bowed low to the two sword masters. He then began to explain what he had seen.

    "The first of the swords was by all accounts a fine sword, however it is a blood thirsty, evil blade, as it does not discriminate as to who or what it will cut. It may just as well be cutting down butterflies as severing heads. The second was by far the finer of the two, as it does not needlessly cut that which is innocent and undeserving."

zlin328
Sword of Truth
Sword of Truth

The Sword of Truth is a sword that is carried by the Seeker of Truth. The sword has the power to cut through anything perceived as the enemy while not harming a friend. The only exception to this was a sword forged from 100 bloody tips of the armory of the Palace of the Prophets. The Sword of Truth draws on the rage of the one wielding it, but can be turned white and, when used with love and forgiveness, can slay even a friend. However, only the true Seeker can turn the blade of the Sword of Truth white.

In order to use the blade, the wielder must be able to release their anger. If they are not able to release their anger the sword will still work but the price may be their life. The Sword of Truth gives the Seeker a test of pain the first time the Seeker kills with the sword. After many years of usage, the sword wears the Seeker down and eventually turns the wielder into a shadow (or monster) of him/her former self. Only the true Seeker, the one who can turn the blade white, will not wear down in this fashion and remain as he/she is.

zlin337
Tyrfing
Tyrfing

Svafrlami  was the king of Gardariki, and Odin's grandson. He managed to trap the Dwarves  Dvalinn  and Durin when they had left the rock where they dwelt, and forced them to forge a sword with a golden hilt that would never miss a stroke, would never rust and would cut through stone and iron as easily as through clothes. The Dwarves made the sword, and it shone and gleamed like fire. However, in revenge they cursed it so that it would kill a man every time it was drawn and that it would be the cause of three great evils. They finally cursed it so that it would also kill Svafrlami himself. When Svafrlami heard the curses he tried to slay Dvalin, but the Dwarf disappeared into the rock and the sword was driven deep into it, though missing its victim. Svafrlami was killed by the berserker  Arngrim  who took the sword in his turn. After Arngrim, it was worn by Angantyr  and his eleven brothers. They were all slain at Sams√∏, by the champion Hjalmar, and his sworn brother Orvar-Odd; but Hjalmar, being wounded by Tyrfing, has only time to sing his death-song before he dies, and asks Orvar-Odd to bring his body to Ingeborg  at Uppsala. Angantyr's daughter, Hervor (by his wife Tofa) is brought up as a bond-maid, in ignorance of her parentage. When at last she learns it, she arms herself as a shieldmaiden, and goes to Munarvoe in Sams√∏, in quest of the dwarf-cursed weapon. She finds it and marries Hofund. They have two sons, Heidrek and Angantyr. Hervor secretly gave her son the sword Tyrfing. While Angantyr and Heidrek walked, Heidrek wanted to have a look at the sword. Since he had unsheathed it, the curse the Dwarves had put on the sword made Heidrek kill his brother Angantyr. Heidrek became king of the Goths. During a voyage, Heidrek camped at the Carpathians (Harva√∞a fj√∂llum, cf. Grimm's law). He was accompanied by eight mounted thralls, and when Heidrek slept at night, the thralls broke into his tent and took Tyrfing and slew Heidrek. This was the last one of Tyrfing's three evil deeds. Heidrek's son Angantyr  caught the thralls, killed them and reclaimed the magic sword, and the curse had ceased.

The Sword of Shannara
The Sword of Shannara

During the Second War of the Races, the sword was forged by Urprox Screl at the behest of Bremen. Rumored to be the finest smith in all the Southland, Screl put that to the test during the forging, and with aid from an Old World formula provided by the outcast Cogline and the magic of the Druid Bremen he managed to forge it. The Eilt Druin medallion was fused into the hilt, and the truth of Druids past was infused within the weapon. The sword's power confronts any who touch it with the absolute truth about themselves.

Eternal Sword

Dragonslicer
Dragonslicer

The Sword of Heroes, as Dragonslicer is known, is certainly one of the least-feared Swords... one of those least feared by humans, that is. To face Dragonslicer in combat is simply to face a Sword of exceptional quality yet no real magic. Its magic is very specialized, but it has a power rarely seen elsewhere in the world of the Swords -- the ability to slice dragon scales (and other parts) as if they were the hide (and flesh) of a much lesser, non-magical reptile -- and this, in addition to its other "talent", makes the wielder a natural for slaying dragons, but gives no edge when fending off anything else. These limitations to its usefulness keep Dragonslicer from being in great demand among the more power-hungry. If they can acquire it, so much the better, but what have kings and armies to fear from the Sword of Heroes?

Keyblade
Keyblade

As the name implies, in combat, Keyblades are used in a manner similar to swords. Despite the fact that most possess no actual blade, Keyblades still make efficient combat weapons. The origins of the Keyblades is, thus far, unclear. The special qualities of the wielders are given vague explanation of the Keyblades' power, but none have shown where the Keyblades originated, how they are created, or what their original purpose might have been. One legend mentioned in Kingdom Hearts states that the Keyblade master saved the world, while another said he wrought chaos and destruction upon it. While these legends may appear to contradict themselves, it can be assumed that the Keyblade master chooses how to use the Keyblade, whether for good or evil. The Keyblades are known throughout the worlds as a unique and powerful weapons. In Atlantica, King Triton and Ursula both knew of the Keyblades and their powers. King Triton did not want Sora to seal the Keyhole because he thought that the Keyblade would send his world into chaos, while Ursula knew that it gave the ability for the one who wields it to travel around the worlds. All Keyblades shown have the same distinguishing features that are modeled after a key: a guard with a handle, a hilt and a blade with some type of a "sharp point" that gives it a cutting ability, which comes from the grooves and teeth of a real key.

zlin383
Soul Caliber
Soul Caliber

Soul Calibur is the spirit sword created to combat Soul Edge. Algol, the king that once wielded Soul Edge and lost his son because of the demonic sword, vowed to create a holy sword from the purified shards of Soul Edge that would oppose the evil sword, being its equal in strength and opposite in intent. Algol enlisted the help of the greatest sage in the land, who used purified fragments of the cursed sword to forge a new spirit sword, to be known as "Soul Calibur". After many failed attempts, the holy sword was born when Algol sacrificed himself to complete the ritual. However, the sword that was created was far from good due to Algol's thirst for power, and it was extremely similar in nature to Soul Edge. Nonetheless, the tribe that was tasked with guarding the sword slowly purified it to the point that it could be considered a holy weapon, while keeping dormant the dark soul that rested within the sword. The guardians lived in seclusion, passing the sword from generation to generation in secret. Whenever a warrior vowed to take on Soul Edge on his own, Soul Calibur appeared to prevent the cursed sword from causing any more damage. Soul Calibur finally appeared, somehow transformed into a different shape, as one of the Ling-Sheng Su Temple treasures.
Soul Caliber

Soul Calibur is the spirit sword created to combat Soul Edge. Algol, the king that once wielded Soul Edge and lost his son because of the demonic sword, vowed to create a holy sword from the purified shards of Soul Edge that would oppose the evil sword, being its equal in strength and opposite in intent. Algol enlisted the help of the greatest sage in the land, who used purified fragments of the cursed sword to forge a new spirit sword, to be known as "Soul Calibur". Soul Calibur finally appeared, somehow transformed into a different shape, as one of the Ling-Sheng Su Temple treasures.

zlink1
Master Sword
The Master Sword, Bastard Sword +4

  Also known as the "The Blade of Evil's Bane",  the Master Sword has the power to "repel evil", which enables it to overcome powerful dark magic and evil beings. It was forged by the Sages of Hyrule by order of the three goddesses just before the Imprisoning War.
  The blade cross-section is hexagonal with no fuller. On the flats of the blade near the hilt is a Triforce symbol, etched into the steel in gold. It has a blue and purple curved crossguard in the shape of a pair of wings with a small yellow jewel where it meets the hilt. The hilt is padded red with a non-ornate blue pommel.
  The sword can only be wielded by a descendant of the Knights of Hyrule. In fact, only a Hylian Elf who carries their bloodline is capable of fighting with this weapon.
  Pulled from an altar hidden deep within the Lost Woods by the Sages led by Sahasrahla, it was moved to an even more protected hiding place; deep within the vaults and dungeons of the Temple of Time until another one worthy of its powers could be found.
  Indeed, no evil can stand its sight nor stain its sharp blade; darkness scurries from its touch and even the most powerful of daemons with the blackest of hearts can be struck with it. Because of its magical ability to repel evil, the sword also allows its wielder to face untold evils without fear of them or their powers.
  The sword also doubles as a key to the Sacred Realm, and can be used to time-travel

zlink25
Golden Girdle of Gaea 
Golden Girdle of Gaea 

when the Themyscirian Amazons were created by the Olympian gods, they assigned Hippolyta and Antiope to rule as co-queens to the new nation. They gave each of the Amazon queens a Golden Girdle of Gaea, which were made from the original girdle belonging to the Earth goddess. The belts provided the two queens with enhanced strength and heightened their other abilities.

Eventually the demi-god Heracles was successful in stealing Hippolyta's belt at the urging of his half-brother Ares. After denouncing the Olympian gods for perceived false judgement, Antiope gave Hippolyta her girdle and left the Amazon nation with a group of faithful Amazons. They later retrieved Hippolyta's stolen belt from Theseus, one of Hercules' companions, and kept it as an heirloom until it was lost for good later on.

Aegis Shield
Aegis Shield

The aegis, as stated in the Iliad, is the shield of Pallas Athena or Zeus, which according to Homer was fashioned by Hephaestus. Athena lent the Aegis to the legendary hero Perseus, to battle the dreaded Medusa. A Gorgon with steely scales and snakes for hair, Medusa was so frightening to behold that those who viewed her directly turned to stone. Perseus slew Medusa by watching her reflection in the Aegis‚Äô polished surface. Forever after, the shield also became adorned with four snakes in place of the gold tassels, representing fear, flight, force and pursuit, again enhancing the shield‚Äôs mystic impenetrable powers.
